                  def proxy_to_supabase(endpoint, method: :get, params: {}, body: nil)
          
      149. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    149. 
            
            

            

                    supabase_url = ENV['SUPABASE_URL'] || 'http://localhost:54321'
          
      150. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    150. 
            
            

            

                    supabase_key = ENV['SUPABASE_ANON_KEY'] || 'your-anon-key'
          
      151. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    151. 
            
            

            

                    
          
      152. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    152. 
            
            

            

                    url = "#{supabase_url}/rest/v1#{endpoint}"
          
      153. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    153. 
            
            

            

                    
          
      154. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    154. 
            
            

            

                    headers = {
          
      155. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    155. 
            
            

            

                      'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
          
      156. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    156. 
            
            

            

                      'apikey' => supabase_key,
          
      157. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    157. 
            
            

            

                      'Authorization' => "Bearer #{current_user&.supabase_token || supabase_key}"
          
      158. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    158. 
            
            

            

                    }
          
      159. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    159. 
            
            

            

                    
          
      160. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    160. 
            
            

            

                    # URL
          
      161. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    161. 
            
            

            

                    if params.present? && method == :get
          
      162. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    162. 
            
            

            

                      url += "?#{params.to_query}"
          
      163. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    163. 
            
            

            

                    end
          
      164. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    164. 
            
            

            

                    
          
      165. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    165. 
            
            

            

                    begin
          
      166. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    166. 
            
            

            

                      response = case method
          
      167. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    167. 
            
            

            

                                 when :get
          
      168. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    168. 
            
            

            

                                   HTTParty.get(url, headers: headers)
          
      169. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    169. 
            
            

            

                                 when :post
          
      170. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    170. 
            
            

            

                                   HTTParty.post(url, headers: headers, body: body.to_json)
          
      171. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    171. 
            
            

            

                                 when :patch
          
      172. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    172. 
            
            

            

                                   HTTParty.patch(url, headers: headers, body: body.to_json)
          
      173. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    173. 
            
            

            

                                 when :delete
          
      174. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    174. 
            
            

            

                                   HTTParty.delete(url, headers: headers)
          
      175. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    175. 
            
            

            

                                 else
          
      176. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    176. 
            
            

            

                                   raise "Unsupported HTTP method: #{method}"
          
      177. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    177. 
            
            

            

                                 end
          
      178. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    178. 
            
            

            

                      
          
      179. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    179. 
            
            

            

                      if response.success?
          
      180. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    180. 
            
            

            

                        render json: response.parsed_response
          
      181. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    181. 
            
            

            

                      else
          
      182. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    182. 
            
            

            

                        render json: { error: "Supabase API error: #{response.code}" }, status: response.code
          
      183. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    183. 
            
            

            

                      end
          
      184. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    184. 
            
            

            

                    rescue => e
          
      185. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    185. 
            
            

            

                      Rails.logger.error "Supabase API error: #{e.message}"
          
      186. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    186. 
            
            

            

                      render json: { error: "Internal server error" }, status: :internal_server_error
          
      187. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    187. 
            
            

            

                    end
          
      188. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    188. 
            
            

            

                  end
          
      189. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    189. 
            
            

            

                end

              end

                  def search

                      # Supabase

                      if params[:use_supabase] == 'true'

              def can_read_memo?(memo, user)
          
      221. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    221. 
            
            

            

                return false unless memo && user
          
      222. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    222. 
            
            

            

                # Owner can always read
          
      223. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    223. 
            
            

            

                return true if memo.user_id == user.id
          
      224. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    224. 
            
            

            

                # Public memos can be read by anyone
          
      225. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    225. 
            
            

            

                return true if memo.public_memo? # Assumes enum method public_memo? exists
          
      226. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    226. 
            
            

            

                # Shared memos logic (currently not implemented, so shared are private to owner)
          
      227. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    227. 
            
            

            

                # return true if memo.shared? && memo.is_shared_with?(user)
          
      228. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    228. 
            
            

            

                false # Default to no access
          
      229. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    229. 
            
            

            

              end

              def process_tags(memo, tag_names_string)
          
      238. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    238. 
            
            

            

                return if tag_names_string.blank?
          
      239. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    239. 
            
            

            

            
          
      240. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    240. 
            
            

            

                target_tag_names = tag_names_string.split(',').map(&:strip).reject(&:blank?).map(&:downcase).uniq
          
      241. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    241. 
            
            

            

            
          
      242. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    242. 
            
            

            

                return if target_tag_names.empty?
          
      243. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    243. 
            
            

            

            
          
      244. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    244. 
            
            

            

                existing_tags = Tag.where(name: target_tag_names).to_a
          
      245. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    245. 
            
            

            

                existing_tag_names = existing_tags.map(&:name)
          
      246. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    246. 
            
            

            

            
          
      247. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    247. 
            
            

            

                new_tag_names = target_tag_names - existing_tag_names
          
      248. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    248. 
            
            

            

            
          
      249. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    249. 
            
            

            

                created_tags = []
          
      250. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    250. 
            
            

            

                if new_tag_names.any?
          
      251. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    251. 
            
            

            

                  # Tag.find_or_create_by_name handles downcasing and ensures uniqueness correctly.
          
      252. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    252. 
            
            

            

                  # Looping here for new tags is acceptable as find_or_create_by_name is robust.
          
      253. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    253. 
            
            

            

                  # If performance for *brand new* tags in bulk was paramount and Tag model was simpler,
